 On the 5th day of the hearing, the Supreme Court has suggested to All India Muslim Personal Low Board (all India Muslim Personal Law Board) lawyer Kapil Sibal that Muslim women can be given the option of denying them for triple talaq at the time of their marriage? Why don't you pass this proposal that at the time of nikah, the Qazi gives the woman the option that she can ask to refuse three divorces in the nikahnama
 ol india muslim personal laa board kii ore se kapil sibbal ne kaha- ye acha suzav he
 On the other hand, strengthening its stand against triple talaq in the Supreme Court, the Center rejected the argument that triple talaq should be allowed as it has been in practice for centuries
 centre ke sheersh kanoon adhikari mukul rohtagi ne kaha ki talaak nishchit rup se islam kaa ek jaruri hissaa nahin tha or adaalat main ise jari rakhane kii anumati nahin di ja sakati thi, sirf isliye ki vah 1,400 saal puraani parampara he
 In the Supreme Court on triple talaq, AG Mukul Rohatgi said - This case is not about majority vs
 minority
 yah takaraav muslim samudaay main hi he
 CJI Khehar said - but Sibal is saying there is no confrontation
 AG ne kaha- yah takaraav samudaay main hi mahilaon or purushon ke bich he
 The reason for this is that men are earners, they are more educated
 CJI ne poocha-ek baar phir aapse puch rahe hai ki teen talaak radd kar die jaaen to kya hoga AG- If the court gives such a decision, then the government is ready to bring the law
 CJI- yah kaam aap pehle kyon nahin karte? hamaare aadesh kaa intjaar kyon ? AG- The question here is not about the government but what the court does in this case
 AG- halafname main personal lau board khud kah rahaa he ki teen talaak paap he, avaanchhneeya he to aise main saaf he ki teen talaak islam kaa anivaary hissaa nahin he, jo anivaary nahin he use samvidhan dwaara protection kaise diya ja saktaa he? Justice Kurian asked- Kapil Sibal is saying that this is a matter of personal law, it cannot be tested on the test of constitutional rights? AG- teen talaak kaa maamla bhi sanvaidhanik adhikaar ke tahat hi dekha janaa chahie
 Personal laws are also the test of the constitution, as it is not an integral part of religion, hence the right to religious freedom cannot be cited in this case
 CJI khehar ne AG se poocha - board kah rahaa he ki yah 1400 saal puraani parampara he jo aasthaa he
 Shouldn't the court interfere in this? AG- yahaan paramparaon kii baat he to sati pratha, chhooaachhut or vidhwaaon ke punarvivaah jaisi paramparaayen khatm kii gayi Justice Kurian said- you are referring to them but this was done by legislature and finished ag-lekin panrapara ke naam par kya koi bhi samudaay yah kah saktaa he ki narbali hamaari parampara he? Justice Curian - But does this also apply to animal abuse? AG- maine jaanboojhkar narbali kaa zikr kiya he ye sanvaidhanik adhikaron se judaa maamla he
 CJI said- But the constitution also gives right to religious freedom? AG- dharmik swatantraaa kaa adhikaar apane aap main sampurna nahin he
 For example, the constitution says that any person can go to any mosque and read the namaz on his own free will, but no one can go to the Taj Mahal and offer namaz as it is a matter of public order
 isse purv mangalvaar ko AIMPLB board kii ore se kapil sibbal ne kaha- teen talaak 1400 saal puraani pratha he or yah sweekaar kii gai he
 This matter is related to faith, which has been going on for 1400 years, so how is it un-islamic
 jaise maan lijie meri aasthaa ram main he or meraa yah maananaa he ki ram ayodhya main paidaa hue
 If faith cannot be questioned about Ram, then why on triple talaq? This whole matter is related to faith
 personal lau quran or haddees se aayaa he
 Will the court interpret the millions of words written in the Quran? Constitutional ethics and the principle of equality cannot apply to triple talaq as it is a matter of faith
 sunwaayee ke dauraan kapil sibbal ne hinduon se tulana kii
 The constitution recognizes the personal law of all religions
 hinduon main dahej ke khilaaf dahej unmoolan act lekar aae, lekin pratha ke taur par dahej liya ja saktaa he
 In this way, this practice has been preserved among Hindus, while in the case of Muslims, it is being declared unconstitutional
 court ko is maamle main dakhal nahin dena chahie nahin to sawaal uthegaa ki is maamle ko kyon suna ja rahaa he? kyon sangyaan liya gaya
 Sharia is personal law, it cannot be compared on the basis of fundamental rights
 hamen har dharm kii samskruti ko sarankshan dena chahie
 If it is bad then people should be educated about it
 mahasoos karaayaa janaa chahie ki ve galat hai or kanoon bananaa chahie
 Hindus should get protection in every Muslim majority country and in the same way Muslims should get protection in Hindu majority country
 justise courion ne kapil sibbal se kai baar poocha- pavitra quran main pehle se hi talaak kii prakriya bataai gai he to phir teen talaak kii kya jarurat? jab quran main teen talaak kaa koi zikr nahin to ye kahaan se aayaa? is par kapil sibbal ne kaha- quran main teen talaak kaa zikr nahin he, lekin kaha gaya he ki allaah ke massenger kii baat maano
 The practice of three divorces from the Messenger of Allah and his companions began
 ye aasthaa kaa maamla he, court isaki vyakhya nahin kar saktaa
 Justice Kurian said - at least we can find out whether triple talaq is part of faith or not? The comments sunwaayee ke dauraan supreme court ne poocha is mudde par samudaay kuch kyon nahin kar rahaa
 On this, Kapil Sibal said - We are not saying that triple talaq is right
 ye talaak kaa sabase avaanchhneeya tarika he
 We are explaining to everyone not to use it
 ham ye bhi kah rahe hai ki teen talaak permanent nahin he, lekin ham ye nahin chaahate ki koi doosraa hamen bataae ki teen talaak kharaab he
 Only the people of the community will come out of it

 The practice of three divorces from the Messenger of Allah and his companions began
 ye aasthaa kaa maamla he, court isaki vyakhya nahin kar saktaa
 Justice Kurian said - at least we can find out whether triple talaq is part of faith or not? The comments sunwaayee ke dauraan supreme court ne poocha is mudde par samudaay kuch kyon nahin kar rahaa
 On this, Kapil Sibal said - We are not saying that triple talaq is right
 ye talaak kaa sabase avaanchhneeya tarika he
 We are explaining to everyone not to use it
 ham ye bhi kah rahe hai ki teen talaak permanent nahin he, lekin ham ye nahin chaahate ki koi doosraa hamen bataae ki teen talaak kharaab he
 Only the people of the community will come out of it
 bataa den ki is maamle main sunwaayee ke dauraan samvidhan peeth ke sabhi jaj muslimon ke pavitra granth quran kaa angreji anuwaad lekar baithete hai or jirah ke dauraan angreji kii quran se lau board or sarkaar ke tarkon kii vyakhya di jaati he
 CJI Khehar said - but Sibal is saying there is no confrontation
 AG ne kaha- yah takaraav samudaay main hi mahilaon or purushon ke bich he
 The reason for this is that men are earners, they are more educated
 CJI ne poocha-ek baar phir aapse puch rahe hai ki teen talaak radd kar die jaaen to kya hoga AG- If the court gives such a decision, then the government is ready to bring the law
 CJI- yah kaam aap pehle kyon nahin karte? hamaare aadesh kaa intjaar kyon ? AG- The question here is not about the government but what the court does in this case
 AG- halafname main personal lau board khud kah rahaa he ki teen talaak paap he, avaanchhneeya he to aise main saaf he ki teen talaak islam kaa anivaary hissaa nahin he, jo anivaary nahin he use samvidhan dwaara protection kaise diya ja saktaa he? Justice Kurian asked- Kapil Sibal is saying that this is a matter of personal law, it cannot be tested on the test of constitutional rights? AG- teen talaak kaa maamla bhi sanvaidhanik adhikaar ke tahat hi dekha janaa chahie
 Personal laws are also the test of the constitution, as it is not an integral part of religion, hence the right to religious freedom cannot be cited in this case
 CJI khehar ne AG se poocha - board kah rahaa he ki yah 1400 saal puraani parampara he jo aasthaa he
 Shouldn't the court interfere in this? AG- yahaan paramparaon kii baat he to sati pratha, chhooaachhut or vidhwaaon ke punarvivaah jaisi paramparaayen khatm kii gayi Justice Kurian said- you are referring to them but this was done by legislature and finished ag-lekin panrapara ke naam par kya koi bhi samudaay yah kah saktaa he ki narbali hamaari parampara he? Justice Curian - But does this also apply to animal abuse? AG- maine jaanboojhkar narbali kaa zikr kiya he ye sanvaidhanik adhikaron se judaa maamla he
 CJI said- But the constitution also gives right to religious freedom? AG- dharmik swatantraaa kaa adhikaar apane aap main sampurna nahin he
 For example, the constitution says that any person can go to any mosque and read the namaz on his own free will, but no one can go to the Taj Mahal and offer namaz as it is a matter of public order
 isse purv mangalvaar ko AIMPLB board kii ore se kapil sibbal ne kaha- teen talaak 1400 saal puraani pratha he or yah sweekaar kii gai he
 This matter is related to faith, which has been going on for 1400 years, so how is it un-islamic
 jaise maan lijie meri aasthaa ram main he or meraa yah maananaa he ki ram ayodhya main paidaa hue
 If faith cannot be questioned about Ram, then why on triple talaq? This whole matter is related to faith
 personal lau quran or haddees se aayaa he
 Will the court interpret the millions of words written in the Quran? Constitutional ethics and the principle of equality cannot apply to triple talaq as it is a matter of faith
 sunwaayee ke dauraan kapil sibbal ne hinduon se tulana kii
 The constitution recognizes the personal law of all religions
 hinduon main dahej ke khilaaf dahej unmoolan act lekar aae, lekin pratha ke taur par dahej liya ja saktaa he
 In this way, this practice has been preserved among Hindus, while in the case of Muslims, it is being declared unconstitutional
 court ko is maamle main dakhal nahin dena chahie nahin to sawaal uthegaa ki is maamle ko kyon suna ja rahaa he? kyon sangyaan liya gaya
 Sharia is personal law, it cannot be compared on the basis of fundamental rights
 hamen har dharm kii samskruti ko sarankshan dena chahie
 If it is bad then people should be educated about it
 mahasoos karaayaa janaa chahie ki ve galat hai or kanoon bananaa chahie
 Hindus should get protection in every Muslim majority country and in the same way Muslims should get protection in Hindu majority country
 justise courion ne kapil sibbal se kai baar poocha- pavitra quran main pehle se hi talaak kii prakriya bataai gai he to phir teen talaak kii kya jarurat? jab quran main teen talaak kaa koi zikr nahin to ye kahaan se aayaa? is par kapil sibbal ne kaha- quran main teen talaak kaa zikr nahin he, lekin kaha gaya he ki allaah ke massenger kii baat maano
 The practice of three divorces from the Messenger of Allah and his companions began
 ye aasthaa kaa maamla he, court isaki vyakhya nahin kar saktaa
 Justice Kurian said - at least we can find out whether triple talaq is part of faith or not? The comments sunwaayee ke dauraan supreme court ne poocha is mudde par samudaay kuch kyon nahin kar rahaa
 On this, Kapil Sibal said - We are not saying that triple talaq is right
 ye talaak kaa sabase avaanchhneeya tarika he
 We are explaining to everyone not to use it
 ham ye bhi kah rahe hai ki teen talaak permanent nahin he, lekin ham ye nahin chaahate ki koi doosraa hamen bataae ki teen talaak kharaab he
 Only the people of the community will come out of it
 bataa den ki is maamle main sunwaayee ke dauraan samvidhan peeth ke sabhi jaj muslimon ke pavitra granth quran kaa angreji anuwaad lekar baithete hai or jirah ke dauraan angreji kii quran se lau board or sarkaar ke tarkon kii vyakhya di jaati he
 CJI asked - Once again you are asking what will happen if three divorces are canceled
 AG- agar court aisa faisla detaa he to sarkaar kanoon laane ko taiyaar he
 CJI- Why don't you do this work first? Why wait for our order? AG- yahaan sawaal sarkaar kaa nahin balki ye barkaraar he ki court is maamle main kya karata he
 In the affidavit, the Personal Law Board itself is saying that triple talaq is a sin, undesirable, so it is clear that triple talaq is not an essential part of Islam, which is not mandatory, how can it be protected by the Constitution? justise courion ne poocha- kapil sibbal kah rahe hai ki yah personal lau kaa maamla he ise sanvaidhanik adhikaron kii kasuti par test nahin ja saktaa? ag-triple talaq case should also be looked into under constitutional right
 personal lau bhi samvidhan kii kasuti par test hote hai, kyonki ye dharm kaa abhinn hissaa nahin he isliye is maamle main dharmik swatantraaa ke adhikaar kaa hawala nahin diya ja saktaa
 CJI Khehar asked the AG - The board is saying that this is a 1400 year old tradition which is faith
 isamen court ko dakhal nahin dena chahie? AG- Here is the tradition, traditions like Sati, untouchability and widow remarriage were abolished justise courion ne kaha- aap inkaa zikr kar rahe hai lekin ye to vidhayika dwaara kanoon banaakar khatm kiya gaya AG- But in the name of tradition, can any community say that human sacrifice is our tradition? justise courion- lekin kya yah baat pashuon kii bali main bhi lagu hoti he? AG- i have deliberately mentioned narcotics this is a matter related to constitutional rights
 CJI ne kaha- lekin samvidhan dharmik swatantraaa kaa adhikaar bhi detaa he? AG- Right to religious freedom is not absolute in itself
 udhaaharan ke taur par samvidhan kahata he ki koi bhi shaks apni marji se kisi bhi masjid main jaakar namaaj pard saktaa he, lekin koi tajmahal main jaakar namaaj nahin pard saktaa kyonki ye public order kaa maamla he
 Earlier on Tuesday, Kapil Sibal said on behalf of the AIMPLB board - triple talaq is a 1400 year old practice and has been accepted
 yah maamla aasthaa se juda he, jo 1400 saal se chal rahaa he to ye gaiyr-islamic kaise he
 Like suppose i have faith in Rama and i believe that Rama was born in Ayodhya
 agar ram ko lekar aasthaa par sawaal nahin uthaae ja sakate to teen talaak par kyon? yah sara maamla aasthaa se juda he
 Personal law comes from the Quran and Hadith
 kya court quran main likhe lakhon shabdon kii vyakhya karegaa? sanvaidhanik naitikta or samanta kaa siddhant teen talaak par lagu nahin ho saktaa kyonki yah aasthaa kaa vishay he
 During the hearing, Kapil Sibal compared Hindus
 samvidhan sabhi dharmon ke personal lau ko pahchaan detaa he 
 Hindus brought dowry elimination act against dowry, but dowry can be taken as a practice
 is tarah hinduon main is pratha ko sarankshan diya gaya he to vahiin muslim ke maamle main ise ansavaidhanik qaraar diya ja rahaa he
 The court should not interfere in this matter, otherwise the question will arise, why is this case being heard? Why was cognizance taken? shariat personal lau he, isaki tulana moulik adhikaron ke aadhaar par nahin kii ja sakati
 We should preserve the culture of every religion
 agar vah kharaab bhi he to logon ko iske vishay main shikshit karnaa chahie
 It should be realized that they are wrong and should be made law
 har muslim bahusankhyak desh main hinduon ko sarankshan milanaa chahie or usee tarah hindu bahusankhyak desh main muslimon ko sarankshan mili
 Justice Kurian asked Kapil Sibal many times- The process of divorce has already been told in the Holy Quran, so what is the need for triple talaq? When in the Quran there is no mention of triple talaq, where did it come from? On this, Kapil Sibal said- Quran does not mention three divorces, but it has been said that obey the Messenger of Allah
 allaah ke massenger or unke saathiyon se teen talaak kii pratha shuru hui
 It is a matter of faith, the court cannot explain it
 justise courion ne kaha - kam se kam ham ye to pataa laga hi sakate hai ki teen talaak aasthaa kaa hissaa he yaa nahin?tippaniyan During the hearing, the Supreme Court asked why the community was not doing anything on this issue
 is par kapil sibbal ne kaha- ham ye nahin kah rahe ki teen talaak sahi he
 This is the most undesirable method of divorce
 ham sabhi ko samajha rahe hai ki iskaa istemaal naa karen
 We are also saying that triple talaq is not permanent, but we do not want anyone to tell us that triple talaq is bad
 samudaay ke log hi isse baahar niklenge
 Explain that during the hearing in this case, all the judges of the Constitution Bench sit with the English translation of the Holy Book Quran of Muslims and during the arguments, the arguments of the Law Board and the Government are given from the English Quran

AG- Here is the tradition, traditions like Sati, untouchability and widow remarriage were abolished justise courion ne kaha- aap inkaa zikr kar rahe hai lekin ye to vidhayika dwaara kanoon banaakar khatm kiya gaya AG- But in the name of tradition, can any community say that human sacrifice is our tradition? justise courion- lekin kya yah baat pashuon kii bali main bhi lagu hoti he? AG- i have deliberately mentioned narcotics this is a matter related to constitutional rights
 CJI ne kaha- lekin samvidhan dharmik swatantraaa kaa adhikaar bhi detaa he? AG- Right to religious freedom is not absolute in itself
 udhaaharan ke taur par samvidhan kahata he ki koi bhi shaks apni marji se kisi bhi masjid main jaakar namaaj pard saktaa he, lekin koi tajmahal main jaakar namaaj nahin pard saktaa kyonki ye public order kaa maamla he
 Earlier on Tuesday, Kapil Sibal said on behalf of the AIMPLB board - triple talaq is a 1400 year old practice and has been accepted
 yah maamla aasthaa se juda he, jo 1400 saal se chal rahaa he to ye gaiyr-islamic kaise he
 Like suppose i have faith in Rama and i believe that Rama was born in Ayodhya
 agar ram ko lekar aasthaa par sawaal nahin uthaae ja sakate to teen talaak par kyon? yah sara maamla aasthaa se juda he
 Personal law comes from the Quran and Hadith
 kya court quran main likhe lakhon shabdon kii vyakhya karegaa? sanvaidhanik naitikta or samanta kaa siddhant teen talaak par lagu nahin ho saktaa kyonki yah aasthaa kaa vishay he
 During the hearing, Kapil Sibal compared Hindus
 samvidhan sabhi dharmon ke personal lau ko pahchaan detaa he 
 Hindus brought dowry elimination act against dowry, but dowry can be taken as a practice
 is tarah hinduon main is pratha ko sarankshan diya gaya he to vahiin muslim ke maamle main ise ansavaidhanik qaraar diya ja rahaa he
 The court should not interfere in this matter, otherwise the question will arise, why is this case being heard? Why was cognizance taken? shariat personal lau he, isaki tulana moulik adhikaron ke aadhaar par nahin kii ja sakati
 We should preserve the culture of every religion
 agar vah kharaab bhi he to logon ko iske vishay main shikshit karnaa chahie
 It should be realized that they are wrong and should be made law
 har muslim bahusankhyak desh main hinduon ko sarankshan milanaa chahie or usee tarah hindu bahusankhyak desh main muslimon ko sarankshan mili
 Justice Kurian asked Kapil Sibal many times- The process of divorce has already been told in the Holy Quran, so what is the need for triple talaq? When in the Quran there is no mention of triple talaq, where did it come from? On this, Kapil Sibal said- Quran does not mention three divorces, but it has been said that obey the Messenger of Allah
 allaah ke massenger or unke saathiyon se teen talaak kii pratha shuru hui
 It is a matter of faith, the court cannot explain it
 justise courion ne kaha - kam se kam ham ye to pataa laga hi sakate hai ki teen talaak aasthaa kaa hissaa he yaa nahin?tippaniyan During the hearing, the Supreme Court asked why the community was not doing anything on this issue
 is par kapil sibbal ne kaha- ham ye nahin kah rahe ki teen talaak sahi he
 This is the most undesirable method of divorce
 ham sabhi ko samajha rahe hai ki iskaa istemaal naa karen
 We are also saying that triple talaq is not permanent, but we do not want anyone to tell us that triple talaq is bad
 samudaay ke log hi isse baahar niklenge
 Explain that during the hearing in this case, all the judges of the Constitution Bench sit with the English translation of the Holy Book Quran of Muslims and during the arguments, the arguments of the Law Board and the Government are given from the English Quran
 justise courion ne poocha- kapil sibbal kah rahe hai ki yah personal lau kaa maamla he ise sanvaidhanik adhikaron kii kasuti par test nahin ja saktaa? ag-triple talaq case should also be looked into under constitutional right
 personal lau bhi samvidhan kii kasuti par test hote hai, kyonki ye dharm kaa abhinn hissaa nahin he isliye is maamle main dharmik swatantraaa ke adhikaar kaa hawala nahin diya ja saktaa
 CJI Khehar asked the AG - The board is saying that this is a 1400 year old tradition which is faith
 isamen court ko dakhal nahin dena chahie? AG- Here is the tradition, traditions like Sati, untouchability and widow remarriage were abolished justise courion ne kaha- aap inkaa zikr kar rahe hai lekin ye to vidhayika dwaara kanoon banaakar khatm kiya gaya AG- But in the name of tradition, can any community say that human sacrifice is our tradition? justise courion- lekin kya yah baat pashuon kii bali main bhi lagu hoti he?  samvidhan sabhi dharmon ke personal lau ko pahchaan detaa he 
 Hindus brought dowry elimination act against dowry, but dowry can be taken as a practice

 The court should not interfere in this matter, otherwise the question will arise, why is this case being heard? Why was cognizance taken? shariat personal lau he, isaki tulana moulik adhikaron ke aadhaar par nahin kii ja sakati

 agar vah kharaab bhi he to logon ko iske vishay main shikshit karnaa chahie

 har muslim bahusankhyak desh main hinduon ko sarankshan milanaa chahie or usee tarah hindu bahusankhyak desh main muslimon ko sarankshan mili
 Justice Kurian asked Kapil Sibal many times- The process of divorce has already been told in the Holy Quran, so what is the need for triple talaq? When in the Quran there is no mention of triple talaq, where did it come from? On this, Kapil Sibal said- Quran does not mention three divorces, but it has been said that obey the Messenger of Allah
 allaah ke massenger or unke saathiyon se teen talaak kii pratha shuru hui
 It is a matter of faith, the court cannot explain it
 justise courion ne kaha - kam se kam ham ye to pataa laga hi sakate hai ki teen talaak aasthaa kaa hissaa he yaa nahin?tippaniyan During the hearing, the Supreme Court asked why the community was not doing anything on this issue
 is par kapil sibbal ne kaha- ham ye nahin kah rahe ki teen talaak sahi he
 This is the most undesirable method of divorce
 ham sabhi ko samajha rahe hai ki iskaa istemaal naa karen
 We are also saying that triple talaq is not permanent, but we do not want anyone to tell us that triple talaq is bad
 samudaay ke log hi isse baahar niklenge
 Explain that during the hearing in this case, all the judges of the Constitution Bench sit with the English translation of the Holy Book Quran of Muslims and during the arguments, the arguments of the Law Board and the Government are given from the English Quran
 AG- teen talaak kaa maamla bhi sanvaidhanik adhikaar ke tahat hi dekha janaa chahie
 Personal laws are also the test of the constitution, as it is not an integral part of religion, hence the right to religious freedom cannot be cited in this case
 CJI khehar ne AG se poocha - board kah rahaa he ki yah 1400 saal puraani parampara he jo aasthaa he
 Shouldn't the court interfere in this? AG- yahaan paramparaon kii baat he to sati pratha, chhooaachhut or vidhwaaon ke punarvivaah jaisi paramparaayen khatm kii gayi Justice Kurian said- you are referring to them but this was done by legislature and finished ag-lekin panrapara ke naam par kya koi bhi samudaay yah kah saktaa he ki narbali hamaari parampara he? Justice Curian - But does this also apply to animal abuse? AG- maine jaanboojhkar narbali kaa zikr kiya he ye sanvaidhanik adhikaron se judaa maamla he
 CJI said- But the constitution also gives right to religious freedom? AG- dharmik swatantraaa kaa adhikaar apane aap main sampurna nahin he
 For example, the constitution says that any person can go to any mosque and read the namaz on his own free will, but no one can go to the Taj Mahal and offer namaz as it is a matter of public order
 isse purv mangalvaar ko AIMPLB board kii ore se kapil sibbal ne kaha- teen talaak 1400 saal puraani pratha he or yah sweekaar kii gai he
 This matter is related to faith, which has been going on for 1400 years, so how is it un-islamic
 jaise maan lijie meri aasthaa ram main he or meraa yah maananaa he ki ram ayodhya main paidaa hue
 If faith cannot be questioned about Ram, then why on triple talaq? This whole matter is related to faith
 personal lau quran or haddees se aayaa he
 Will the court interpret the millions of words written in the Quran? Constitutional ethics and the principle of equality cannot apply to triple talaq as it is a matter of faith
 sunwaayee ke dauraan kapil sibbal ne hinduon se tulana kii
 The constitution recognizes the personal law of all religions
 hinduon main dahej ke khilaaf dahej unmoolan act lekar aae, lekin pratha ke taur par dahej liya ja saktaa he
 In this way, this practice has been preserved among Hindus, while in the case of Muslims, it is being declared unconstitutional
 court ko is maamle main dakhal nahin dena chahie nahin to sawaal uthegaa ki is maamle ko kyon suna ja rahaa he? kyon sangyaan liya gaya
 Sharia is personal law, it cannot be compared on the basis of fundamental rights
 hamen har dharm kii samskruti ko sarankshan dena chahie
 If it is bad then people should be educated about it
 mahasoos karaayaa janaa chahie ki ve galat hai or kanoon bananaa chahie
 Hindus should get protection in every Muslim majority country and in the same way Muslims should get protection in Hindu majority country
 justise courion ne kapil sibbal se kai baar poocha- pavitra quran main pehle se hi talaak kii prakriya bataai gai he to phir teen talaak kii kya jarurat? jab quran main teen talaak kaa koi zikr nahin to ye kahaan se aayaa? is par kapil sibbal ne kaha- quran main teen talaak kaa zikr nahin he, lekin kaha gaya he ki allaah ke massenger kii baat maano
 The practice of three divorces from the Messenger of Allah and his companions began
 ye aasthaa kaa maamla he, court isaki vyakhya nahin kar saktaa
 Justice Kurian said - at least we can find out whether triple talaq is part of faith or not? The comments sunwaayee ke dauraan supreme court ne poocha is mudde par samudaay kuch kyon nahin kar rahaa
 On this, Kapil Sibal said - We are not saying that triple talaq is right
 ye talaak kaa sabase avaanchhneeya tarika he
 We are explaining to everyone not to use it
 ham ye bhi kah rahe hai ki teen talaak permanent nahin he, lekin ham ye nahin chaahate ki koi doosraa hamen bataae ki teen talaak kharaab he
 Only the people of the community will come out of it
 bataa den ki is maamle main sunwaayee ke dauraan samvidhan peeth ke sabhi jaj muslimon ke pavitra granth quran kaa angreji anuwaad lekar baithete hai or jirah ke dauraan angreji kii quran se lau board or sarkaar ke tarkon kii vyakhya di jaati he

 What has been the history of the Nashik Lok Sabha seat
 
 
 nasik loksabhaa seat par sabase pehle 1952 main congress ne jeet hasil kii thi
 Yes
 ech deshpandey saansad chune gaye the
 After this, in 1957 Bhaurao Kishenji Gaikwad won elections from the Schedule Caste Federation
 1962 main dobaaraa ji
 H
 Deshpande became an MP by winning the election
 lekin unke nidhan ke baad 1963 main yahaan dobaaraa upachunaav hue
 Yashwant Rao Chavan was elected as an MP
 bataa den ki yashavanth raav chavaan maharashtra ke pehle mukhyamantri the, wo up-pradhanmantri bhi rahe
 In the subsequent elections in 1967, B
 aar kawade saansad bane, wo 1971 main dobaaraa jite
 In 1977, the victory of the Congress was broken by Vitthal Rao Hande
 wo shetakari kaamgaar paksh kii tikat se saansad chune gaye
 But the Congress returned in the 1980 election
 pratap raav vaagh saansad bane
 After that, in 1984, Muralidhar Mane won elections from the Congress
 jab pehali baar jiti bijepi
 
 
 The BJP won the Nashik Lok Sabha seat for the first time in 1989
 daulataraav aher saansad chune gaye
 But in the same year, the equation changed here and the Congress returned in the 1991 elections
 shivasena or ensipi kii entry
 
 
 
 1990 ke dashak main congress kii pakad nasik loksabhaa seat par kamjor padane lagi
 The effect of which appeared in the 1996 Lok Sabha elections
 yahaan shivasena ne pehali baar jeet hasil kii
 Rajaram Godse was elected MP
 lekin 1998 ke chunaav main congress kii waapas entry hui or madhav patil chunaav jite
 After this, the Congress was completely eliminated from the Nashik Lok Sabha seat
 1999 main shivasena ke uttamrao dhikale chunaav jite
 Then in 2004 NCP came to power for the first time here
 devidas aanandarav pingale chunaav jite
 In 2009 NCP managed to win the election again
 chagan bhujabal ke bhattije samir bhujabal saansad bane
 Then after the 2014 Lok Sabha elections Hemant Godse of Shiv Sena won here
 kya he vidhansabha siton kii sthiti

 ' The Modi government is going to introduce a new Lokayukta bill in Gujarat on Tuesday
 is bill ke mutabik lokayukta kii niyukti kaa aakhri faisla mukhyamantri kaa hoga
 This would directly mean that the CM of the state would appoint Lokayukta as per his choice
 nae vidheyak main do nae lokayukta or chaar up lokayukta kaa bhi praavdhaan kiya ja rahaa he
 The appointment of Lokayukta through Governor Kamala Beniwal was challenged by the Modi government of Gujarat in the Supreme Court, but it was rejected by the court
 samvidhan ke anusaar rajya main lokayukta kii niyukti rajyapal rajya hai court ke chif justise ke paraamarsh par karata he lekin is bill ke baad gujarat main lokayukta kii niyukti karne ke liye siem se paraamarsh lenaa hi hoga
 Lokayukta has been appointed in 18 of the 28 states of the country
 baaki rajya ise lagu karne main thodi dhilaai barat rahe hai

 ise aaj yani 18 april ko maharashtra main aadhikarik taur par launch kiya jayega

 ye keemten petrol or CNG verient ke liye kramash: 2
 63 lakhs and 2
 83 lakh rupee he
 Today the company can disclose the prices and registration type (commercial or personal) for some more cities
 pichley saal november tak quadricikal ko keval commercial yuj ke liye hi register kiya ja saktaa tha
 However this changed when the Ministry of Road Transport and Highways (morth) included quadricycles in the 'non-transport' category of vehicles
 bajaj ne pehle ye jaankaree di thi ki Qute ko commercial yuj ke liye bharat ke 20 rajyon or privet yuj ke liye 15 rajyon main register kiya ja saktaa he
 However, the company is also planning to expand it to other cities in India
 nai list kaa khulaasa aaj kiya ja saktaa he
 Despite the car look, the Bajaj Qute is not a car
 petrol Qute kaa vajan 452 kilogram or CNG Qute kaa vajan 504 kilogram he

 In this, fiber doors have been given instead of metal

 In a press release issued on March 14, 108 economists and sociologists around the world appealed to the government to restore the autonomy and credibility of their statistics organizations in India
 haalanki, media main is apil kii kaaphi prashansa hui phir bhi kuch logon ne ise sarkaar kii saakh giraane kii suniyojit koshish maanate hue ise rajnatik rup se prerit bataaya
 Economic data are public goods: using them for one person neither prevents another from using them, nor reduces their importance to others
 haalanki aankadon ke saath rajnatik chhedchhad kii sambhaavnaaon ko khatm karne ke liye hi sankhyikee sansthaanon ko swaittata di gai he or unke kaamkaaj kii nigaraanee swatantra visheshgy sanghathan karte hai evam unke aankadon ko ek tay calendar ke mutabik jari kiya jaataa he
 India first institutionalized this work through the establishment of the Central Statistics Office (CSO) and the National Sample Survey Office (NSSO), applying the statistical sample collection principle first to collect socio-economic data
 haalanki, unke tareekon or nateezon ko lekar bahes hoti rahi he, phir bhi in sanghathanon par rajnatik pakshpaat kaa aarope nahin laga tha
 Recently, two important economical indicators — GDP and total employment — came under suspicion
 saal 2015 main aadhaar-varsh sanshodhan ke baad sanshodhit jidipi aankadon par bade paimaane par sawaal uthaae gaye the kyonki unke mutabik, vruddhi daren pehle jari aankadon kii tulana main bahut oonchi hone ke saath hi anya vrahat sahasanyoji aankadon se mail nahin khaati thim
 Since then, the data released almost every time has led to more problems related to the GDP revision, raising questions about changes in the data collection and preparation process and the use of new databases
 do mote udhaahranh nae aadhaar-varsh vaali jidipi se pichley varshon kii jidipi kii nai sanshodhit prakriyaaon or mulyon ke aadhaar par punarganana se do virdohi or alag-alag pravritiyon vaali vruddhi-daren saamne aati hai
 a series has been prepared by another official organization, the National Statistical Commission (NSC), according to which the estimated growth rates of the last decade are higher than the growth rates shown in the previous series; The second series has been prepared by the CSO according to which the projected growth rates for the same period are lower than the rates of the old series
 do aadhikarik sanghathanon ke aise alag-alag dishaao vaale anumaanon or sarkaar ke siesao ke anumaanon ko sweekaar karne ke faisle ne in sanghathanon kii vishwasaneeyata ko gahari chot pahunchaai he
 The amendment to increase the GDP growth rate for the year 2016-17 is also being viewed with suspicion
 vah notebandi kaa saal tha or adhiktar arthshaastri is baat se sahamat hai ki us varsh utpaadan main vruddhi par bura asar padaa tha
 The outgoing Chief Economic Advisor Arvind Subrahmanyam called it 'economic destruction'
 antarrashtriya mudra kosh (iemef) kii mukhya arthshaastri gita gopinath ne ek saajha academik shodhpatr main tark diya tha ki notebandi se us varsh jidipi vruddhi dar main lagbhag do fisadi kii kami ai hogi
 Nevertheless, the revised figures show the growth rate that year at the highest level of 8
 2 fisadi par dikhaa rahe hai!san 1972-73 se panchavarshiya rojgaar-berogari surveykshan (iues) desh main rojgaar dashaon par vistrut aankade dete rahe hai
 Multilevel samples of one lakh families are taken in it
 pichhlaa aisa surveykshan 2011-12 main hua tha
 In 2017-18, this survey was replaced by the Recurrent Labor Force Survey (PLFS)
 nae surveykshan kii aakalpana main badlaav karte hue ise shahari shram bazaar ko zyada vyapaktaa se grahan karne par kendrit kiya gaya, phir bhi, in aankadon ko rojgaar-berogari surveykshan parinaamon ke saath tulana-yogya rakhaa janaa tha
 But in December 2018, the government stopped the PLFS data from being released as per schedule
 dabaai gai report se chhan kar baahar aae aankadon se pataa chalaa ki 2017-18 main berogari kii dar pichley 45 saal main sarvaadhik thi
 This further confirmed those fears that political interference in the country's statistical system has increased so much that it cannot be ignored
